<rate>5< /rate>< review>
I enjoyed Three Seasons very much. I am vegetarian and my family shared 4 dishes- all of which ranged from good to excellent. The crispy veg roll was good(taro in it made it special). The noodles and fried tofu were really good. The noodles had lots of sprouts and the flavor was delicious. The fried tofu was crispy and the coating was very well seasoned. Now comes the amazing veg. curry- I was skeptical but  quite honestly blown away by how well this dish was. Firstly they had very interesting vegetables- brussels sprouts, okra, 2 kinds of cauliflower- all of which were cooked just right, good quality veggies and absorbed the curry flavor. Needless to say, I'll be back. The ambiance was also very pleasant. You get what you pay for!(would reduce half star for the salad that came with crispy rolls which smelled a bit of fish sauce- but this was on the side).</review>

<review>I heard Three Seasons was good from a friend but was pretty disappointed after dining here.  The food was just OK but was extremely overpriced.  Even if portions are small, I would expect the restaurant to compensate in taste or quality. Unfortunately, this is there Three Seasons fell short.

I won't complain about the $9 for 6 oysters special -- not a bad deal, but, the rolls were definitely overpriced.  We shared the traditional spring rolls and crispy rolls which were not outstanding.  I've definitely had superior or comparable rolls for about half the price and hole-in-the-wall Vietnamese places. We also had the garlic noodles which were pretty bland and the chicken salad which was nothing special.

Service was ok -- I think our waitress forgot about us after we ordered and we had to flag down another server to order more food.  This place has a beautiful atmosphere and the outdoor seating was lovely but I'm afraid I won't be back due anytime soon.  I'm not willing to pay extra just for a nice atmosphere so hopefully they can step up the quality of their dishes.<//review>< pictures>

<user>112704870730510086957< /user><review>Nice ambiance & service. Ambiance is better than at Tamarine - the other Vietnamese fusion place in Palo Alto - for one reason because tables are not so closely spaced. The food continues to be excellent. There are many vegetarian & vegan items. I have had vegetarian spring rolls with shots of asparagus soup or cauliflower bisque (this is a great item), garlic noodles (made with egg but those who have tried it love it), papaya salad (very nice & not to strong in taste like some other places that serve this), curry veggies (very good, not too spicy, a nice variety of vegetables, eggplant in coconut sauce (the best item), Spinach noodles (good), lemon tofu (good), green beans (good), crispy vegetarian rolls (okay), tofu eggplant satay (okay) & spicy okra (okay) Drinks: the virgin guavati & lemonade/passion fruit iced tea were good. Our friends loved the creme brulee but we liked the chocolate fondant as well as the mango sorbet, vanilla sorbet & coconut ice cream. The fried banana was good. The teas & coffees are also nice. The restaurant recently redid its interior - which continues to be elegant in style.<//review></record>

<Review>This used to be a 4 star restaurant for me - I've been here numerous times in the past years - their Valentine's Day dinner, parties of 2 to 6, and even birthdays.  And who can deny that their rolls are good?

But, success has gone to their head and I'm sad to say that they've lost my business.  Why?

- Didn't count my reservation with opentable, causing me to "prove" that I went to the restaurant with open table, which is always a hassle
- Took over an hour to bring us our main courses
- Slow water service, virtually non-existent waiter
- Their portions have gotten smaller, while prices have gone up...their New Zealand 5-spice lamb was one of my favorites, but it's more expensive and smaller than ever.  Really disappointing
- incorrect items were placed on our bill
- Dirty, broken dishes set at our table

Anyway, if you have money to blow, get the rolls and get out.< /Review><resp>None</resp></record></dataset><record>

<username>Ramey Echt< /username><Rating>2</Rating><text>The outdoor space is beautiful and the seating is comfortable and nice.  The inside is nice as well... obviously a historic building of some sort.

The food left A LOT to be desired.  Portions are small, flavors are bland (especially for vietnamese food), and choices aren't that great.  Food presentation was nice. As others have stated, prices are definitely expensive for the quantity and quality of the food.

We had Vegetarian Spring Rolls with a sauce that was nothing to write home about. The asparagus soup shots that came with the dish was a nice touch.  The Chicken Satay was okay, but the peanut sauce totally fell short.  Finally, the grapefruit/jicama salad was a disaster.  Full of jicama, not much grapefruit, and a total of 4 cashews in the dish.  After those disappointing dishes, we gave up.

If you're looking for a nice place to relax and don't care much about the food quality, you will enjoy.  If you're looking for good vietnamese food, I suggest looking elsewhere.<//text>< gmapID>

- Ease of renting. 5‚≠ê 's. We decided late Saturday night to rent a Harley on Sunday. <Review>While visiting from Germany my friend got a day off to have me ride with him in SD county. So I headed to Eagle Rider yesterday evening. I wasn't sure if the trip was gonna happen and a little bit tired after spending all day in LA. So Anitra told me to not sweat it if I'm tired and not 100% sure and come back in the morning. We wanted to start the tour at 9 and Eagle Rider didn't open until 10. However, Anitra told me that she would come in a little earlier to get me on the road. This morning I headed to Eagle Rider after my buddy confirmed and Anitra was there to attend me. She walked me through the process of the rental and took my data, German driver license and my card for payment. Made sure I knew everything I needed about the bike, some routes, and the return. We spend a wonderful day in SD county. I even got a new 2018 Fatboy, the bike I'm actually looking to buy. The bike was impeccable, the ride smooth. Came back at 6:40 PM 20 minutes before closing with a full tank of gas. Anitra was there for the return, as promised. She showed genuine interest in my experience and was very kind and professional. The next time I'm in town I will definitely come back here. Highly recommend!<//Review>< GmapID>

< name>
Emil Cheng<//name>
<Date>1597910069831</Date>< rating>
4</rating>
< Review>
We've been coming to this place a few times a month prior to the COVID-19 pandemic. Now during the pandemic, this is one of the few places we come to when we're tired of cooking at home. Thank goodness that they're still open for to-go orders. Just place your order on the phone and your food will be ready for pick-up in about 15 - 20 mins. Their setup is really easy to maintain social distancing especially with contact-less payment. Their food is consistently good with decent sized portions. Their #20 Yang Chow Fried Rice and #15 Curry are our favorite items. On cold days, their #1 House Bowl and #5 Assorted Seafood noodle soups are great choices.</Review>

<Review>Integrity maybe has integrity but at your own expense. Let me elaborate:
Integrity are not flexible, means, if insurance asked them to lower their hourly rate a little bit or lower their price to be in-line with other body shops, they will not. That means, you will be responsible for any extra Dollar amount  not approved by the insurance, which also include any damages have not been discovered yet.
It happens to me. Their hourly rate is $95; the insurance asked them to change it to $90; they refused. So for $30, they lost my business.
Who wants to pay money for damage done by another person to his/her own car. Is it enough trouble the person is going through ????

Nice clean place with consistency theme of snowflakes.  Taiwanese ice meets bubble tea meets hand rolled ice cream.  Visual appeal of hand rolled ice cream with open air style kitchen looks good.  We arrived around 2:30 so we didn't see anyone getting food but the menu looked simple and good.  Hand rolled ice cream looked and tasted good just like the presentation. I guess it must be easy to take the TIME out of your busy day to write a NEGATIVE review, but not a GOOD one. So I'm here to make a difference and writing a GREAT review for this Urgent Care facility... Because I happen to have the day off today (and have the time) because I'm INJURED. :-)
So yesterday at about 5:30PM I stabbed myself in the right foot with a pitchfork. Yes, in San Diego! :-) (We use pitchforks to go clam-digging at Silver Strand on the weekend and I was taking them out of my trunk and one slipped and almost went right through my foot to the bottom-ugh).
It was a small puncture, but really deep... and it wouldn't stop bleeding. At about 8 PM (as I'm still bleeding out), a girlfriend of mine insisted on taking me to Urgent Care. I found this place on my phone... and I'm sooooo grateful I did.
I called in to see if I could get an appointment and the lady who answered was very polite and said they only take "walk-ins" and there was about an hour wait time. So in we went, signed in, did the paperwork and waited for about an hour just as she said (She also said, "Hey, You're the girl with the pitchfork!" when we arrived :-).
The nurse who took us in the back was AMAZING.
She had an incredible bedside manner, was intelligent, kind, extremely knowledgeable, gentle, informative and witty. Her name was Mary Francis and she was VERY passionate about her profession and her love of caring for people was overwhelmingly obvious. I'm mostly writing this review for her because we need more people like Mary Francis in this world and US HealthWorks should be proud and honored to have her on staff.
Immediately after Mary Francis was done taking my vitals, gently cleaning up my wound and getting me positioned properly for the doctor, Dr. Jennifer White came in. (No waiting) She was a pretty and young doctor, who like most- was serious, professional and calculating. She examined my foot, explained my options and procedures to me, and proceeded to seal my wound with medical glue (as opposed to stitches as she suggested). She then told me about the future care of my foot and what to expect. (She told me that I should stay off of it for a couple days, keep it elevated and dry)... and then told me that someone would be in soon to administer a tetanus shot.
Shortly after she left (maybe 2 minutes later) a young guy came in, gave me a tetanus shot (quick and painless) and I was in home and in bed by 9:45PM.
I can't say enough GOOD things about my experience last night at this Urgent Care Clinic; It was very clean, updated, friendly, inviting, professionally staffed, wait time was "normal" and the staff were extremely professional, efficient, kind, caring, knowledgeable, experienced and fast working. I was in at 8:00PM and out by 9:30PM.
It was a VERY POSITIVE experience, and if I could give US HealthWorks more than 5 stars I would- because they deserve it.< /text>

ALEVE...she gave me aleve for a broken wrist.  Additionally, she did not give me a full report of her initial diagnosis.  Only care instructions.  Every other time i've gone to an urgent care i have gotten a diagnosis report. I feel that from a legal standpoint, its probably best to follow proper procedure when diagnosing patients...

Once I got home I reviewed my papers again and guess what...she forgot my prescription so i had to call, ask for it, then go all the way back there to get it. So... I needed to go to urgent care due to a work related injury. I found that this location was the only one in San Diego that was 24/7 which wasn't too inconvenient, as San Diego isn't so big. As a "walk-in" I arrived about 10:45am and there were maybe 2 other people waiting to be seen. Football was on so that was a plus. I filled out the paper work and 10 minutes after I was in an exam room waiting for the Doc. The Doc was thorough and informative (as should be). The longest wait was after the exam waiting on paperwork but I was out of there by about 12:15pm. Granted this was a Sunday so perhaps I just got lucky on timing but to have everything completed within 1hr 30mins seems very acceptable. The staff seemed nice enough and the facility was clean (also, as it should be). I just  wish I had the doctors "cutejulez" (below) had! Would give 5 stars but am still awaiting follow up for ultrasound 3 days later.<//review>
